 '' The caves of Ajanta bear sculpture and paintings inspired by Buddhism and filled with their compassionate feelings, reflecting the exquisite precious times of art in human history
 buddha tathaa jain sampradaay dwaara banaai gai ye gufaaen sajaavati rup se taraashi gai hai

 rangon kaa rachanaatmak upyog or vichaaron kii swatantraaa ke upyog se in gufaaon kii tasveeron main ajanta ke andar jo maanav or jantu rup chitrit kiye gaye hai, unhen kalatmak rachanaatmakataa kaa ek ucch str mana ja saktaa he

 in par bhi taarikh nahin he

 karodon kaa herpher kar rahe the, hawala main lage the

 unhone kaha ki arvind kejariwal ne farji companiyon se chanda liya

 unhone kaha ki in logon ne desh ke saath gaddari kii he

 is sab ke bich bhukh hadtaal ke paanchaven din unki sehat lagaataar bigadati ja rahi he

 lekin, kapil iske liye taiyaar nahin hue the
 They say that the doctors from whose team their report is being taken is not correct
 dilli police kii ek team vahaan lagaataar maujuud he
 Tents have been erected at Mishra's civil lines government residence
 bataa den ki is bhukh hadtaal ke liye unki maang ve pehle hi saaf kar chuke hai
 He has clearly said that till the Aam Aadmi Party does not make public about the foreign visits of its five leaders, the party will go on hunger strike
 jaankaree ke liye bataa den ki kapil mishra jin paanch aam aadmi party ke netaaon ke videsh dauron kii jaankaree saarvajanik karne kii maang kar rahe hai ve paanch naam hai - sanjay singh, raghav chadhdhaa, ashish khetaan, ashutosh or durgesh pathak
 Kapil Mishra alleges that these people have taken personal advantage of foreign tours by misusing party funds
 unhone kaha ki ye paanch kyon videsh gaye the, kiske kharche par gaye the, kahaan ruke the, kisase mili the
 The comments unka kahana he ki party lagaataar pichley kuch samay se yah kah rahi he ki party ke paas fund kii kami he, to aakhir ye netaa kiske kharche par videsh yatraaon kaa laabh le rahe the
 He said that these people also went to Russia
 vahaan kyon gaye the
 There is neither party nor any supporters there
 kapil mishra pehle hi kah chuke hai party sanjay singh videsh dauron par gaye the or logon se tikat aadi ke naam par paise vasuul rahe the
 Not only this, he even alleged that apart from Sanjay Singh, his relatives were also engaged in this work
 bataa den ki punjab chunaav ke dauraan main bhi sanjay singh par is prakaar ke kai aarope lage the
 Let us know that a letter has also been written for Aam Aadmi Party convenor and Delhi Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal
 unhone kaha ki adhiktar chande raat ke 12 baje ke kareeb aae
 Work of blacking out black money was done here
 unhone kaha ki ye farji companiyon banane vaale charted acountint ek he
 The ED has arrested it
 is par notebandi ke dauraan farjivade kaa aarope he
 Mishra alleges that Aam Aadmi Party MLA Shiv Charan Goyal also has a direct link to them
 unhone kaha ki goyal ne apane affidavit main jhooth bolaa
 He made black money white through many fake companies and donated to the party
 raat main chanda dene vaali companiyon main inaki bhi company he
 Two crore party funds were given from their companies
 inke bare main arvind kejariwal ne inkaar kiya tha
 
 
 Kapil Mishra took the name of Deepak Aggarwal
 kaha ki inkaa sidhaa sambandh goyal se kaha jinaki company main ye diarector rahe
 He said that a man named Hemant Kumar is also involved in this mess
 unhone susheel kumaar gupta kaa naam liya or kaha ki inhone goyal ko do karod rupee die the
 Kapil Mishra claimed that these people kept manipulating for donations
 unhone kaha ki in companiyon ne aam aadmi party ko hawala kaa paisa diya
 He also mentioned the party MLA Naresh Yadav Company through which black money was given to the party
 kapil mishra ne daawa kiya ki arvind kejariwal ko apane vidhayakon kii ye sari jaankaree thi
 He said that all these transactions have taken place in the same branch of Axis Bank
 unhone kai or logon ke naam liye jinhone farjivade ke jariye party ko chanda die
 He said hundreds of companies were created at the same address
 kai companiyon ko videshi company bhi dikhaaya gaya

 unhone kaha ki yah aadmi itnaa chanda dene kii ilesibility bhi nahin rakhata

 kapil mishra kaa aarope he ki in logon ko party ke fund kaa durupyog karte hue videsh dauron kaa nijee laabh uthaaya he

And in the end, will this decision secure lic's customers the biggest investment of their lifetime? What is IDBI Bank's situation right now? Currently, the Central Government holds 85% stake in IDBI Bank, one of the 21 state-owned banks in the country
